Page Content
**This electronic version of Chapter 51P of the Dallas City Code is provided to the public as a convenience only.**
**The items posted here are NOT the official versions and should not be relied upon as a substitute for the official versions.**
**The official version of these documents is available at the Office of the Dallas City Secretary or by clicking** [here](https://dallascityhall.com/government/citysecretary/Pages/cMeetings.aspx). 
Best efforts have been used to ensure that this version is accurate and complete. **No official actions may be taken using these versions.** The formatting and pagination of this electronic version may vary from the official version. 
Although updates are made on a regular basis, this electronic version may not contain the most recent regulations. 
This website is sponsored by the City of Dallas Planning and Urban Development Department and maintained by the City Attorney's Office. 
**Editor's note:** _The planned development districts that are not yet posted in this publication are currently being added. The website will be updated continuously. Any Dallas City Council-approved exhibits to the planned development districts contained on this website will be added soon, and when added, may be accessed by clicking on the term "Exhibits" in the Table of Contents._
